6_CD ._.
On_IN a_DT representation_NN from_IN the_DT Collector_NNP of_IN North_NNP Arcot_NNP of_IN the_DT difficulty_NN experienced_VBD in_IN choosing_VBG among_IN a_DT number_NN of_IN rival_JJ applicants_NNS ,_, and_CC of_IN the_DT large_JJ profits_NNS earned_VBN by_IN shopkeepers_NNS ,_, which_WDT ,_, without_IN any_DT risk_NN being_VBG incurred_VBN of_IN pushing_VBG the_DT sale_NN of_IN intoxicating_VBG drugs_NNS ,_, might_MD be_VB diverted_VBN to_TO the_DT public_JJ exchequer_NN ,_, the_DT remedial_JJ measure_NN of_IN enhancing_VBG the_DT license_NN fees_NNS from_IN Rs_NNP ._.
30_CD and_CC 15_CD to_TO Rs_NNP ._.
45_CD and_CC 30_CD in_IN Madras_NNP and_CC the_DT mofussil_NN respectively_RB was_VBD proposed_VBN by_IN the_DT Board_NNP and_CC approved_VBN by_IN Government_NNP to_TO take_VB effect_NN from_IN 1st_CD April_NNP 1890_CD ._.
7_CD ._.
Experience_NN ,_, however_RB ,_, showed_VBD that_IN the_DT demand_NN for_IN these_DT drugs_NNS was_VBD considerably_RB larger_JJR than_IN was_VBD suspected_VBN and_CC that_IN the_DT competition_NN in_IN certain_JJ districts_NNS for_IN the_DT privilege_NN of_IN vend_NN was_VBD ,_, in_IN spite_NN of_IN the_DT enhanced_JJ license_NN fees_NNS ,_, very_RB keen_JJ ,_, in_IN consequence_NN of_IN which_WDT the_DT difficulty_NN of_IN deciding_VBG between_IN the_DT claims_NNS of_IN rival_JJ applicants_NNS was_VBD seriously_RB felt_VBN ._.
The_DT Board_NNP thereupon_IN con-_NN sidered_VBD that_IN the_DT already_RB increased_JJ rate_NN of_IN license_NN fees_NNS might_MD be_VB further_RB enhanced_VBN or_CC that_IN the_DT auction_NN sale_NN system_NN might_MD be_VB adopted_VBN for_IN ascertaining_VBG the_DT true_JJ value_NN of_IN shops_NNS ._.
As_IN the_DT balance_NN of_IN opinion_NN among_IN Collectors_NNS was_VBD against_IN the_DT continuance_NN of_IN the_DT fixed_JJ license_NN fee_NN system_NN as_IN being_VBG entirely_RB inadequate_JJ and_CC unsuited_JJ to_TO the_DT object_NN in_IN view_NN and_CC as_IN sale_NN by_IN auction_NN was_VBD advo-_RB cated_VBN by_IN most_JJS of_IN them_PRP ,_, the_DT Board_NNP recommended_VBD the_DT latter_JJ proposal_NN and_CC suggested_VBD that_IN a_DT minimum_JJ retail_JJ selling_NN price_NN of_IN 4_CD pies_NNS per_IN tola_NN of_IN ganja_NN might_MD be_VB prescribed_VBN as_IN a_DT check_NN against_IN licensees_NNS making_VBG undue_JJ profits_NNS by_IN reduction_NN of_IN prices_NNS and_CC stimulation_NN of_IN sales_NNS ._.

8_CD ._.
The_DT sale_NN of_IN intoxicating_VBG drugs_NNS prepared_VBN from_IN the_DT hemp_NN plant_NN having_VBG thus_RB been_VBN placed_VBN on_IN a_DT satisfactory_JJ footing_NN ,_, the_DT next_JJ question_NN that_WDT engaged_VBD the_DT Board_NNP 's_POS attention_NN was_VBD whether_IN ,_, having_VBG regard_NN to_TO the_DT reported_VBN increase_NN in_IN consumption_NN of_IN ganja_NN ,_, it_PRP would_MD not_RB be_VB justifiable_JJ to_TO impose_VB restrictions_NNS also_RB on_IN the_DT transport_NN and_CC possession_NN of_IN the_DT drug_NN ._.
Closely_RB connected_VBN with_IN this_DT is_VBZ the_DT question_NN of_IN controlling_VBG the_DT cultivation_NN of_IN the_DT hemp_NN plant_NN ._.
The_DT majority_NN of_IN the_DT Collectors_NNS were_VBD for_IN prescribing_VBG the_DT limit_NN of_IN 10_CD or_CC 15_CD tolas_NNS of_IN ganja_NN for_IN possession_NN without_IN license_NN ,_, but_CC the_DT Board_NNP ,_, agreeing_VBG with_IN small_JJ minority_NN that_WDT restrictions_NNS on_IN the_DT cultivation_NN of_IN the_DT plant_NN should_MD precede_VB those_DT on_IN possession_NN ,_, foresaw_VBD that_IN any_DT attempt_NN at_IN controlling_VBG hemp_JJ cultivation_NN would_MD involve_VB the_DT taking_VBG out_IN of_IN a_DT license_NN by_IN every_DT person_NN who_WP had_VBD a_DT plant_NN or_CC two_CD in_IN his_PRP$ garden_NN ._.

(_( a_DT )_) There_EX is_VBZ one_CD uniform_NN system_NN as_IN regards_NNS the_DT sale_NN of_IN hemp_NN drugs_NNS for_IN the_DT province_NN of_IN Sind_NNP ._.

(_( e_NN )_) The_DT cultivator_NN may_MD be_VB considered_VBN to_TO be_VB the_DT wholesale_JJ dealer_NN ,_, and_CC ,_, as_IN already_RB said_VBD ,_, he_PRP requires_VBZ no_DT license_NN ;_: nor_CC does_VBZ the_DT contractor_NN or_CC farmer_NN require_VBP any_DT license_JJ beyond_IN the_DT general_JJ license_NN which_WDT he_PRP buys_VBZ at_IN auction_NN for_IN the_DT right_NN to_TO sell_VB the_DT different_JJ hemp_NN drugs_NNS ._.

CONCLUDING_NN REMARKS_NNP ._.
The_DT method_NN of_IN testing_VBG samples_NNS of_IN hemp_NN drugs_NNS by_IN ascertaining_VBG their_PRP$ physiological_JJ value_NN may_MD be_VB regarded_VBN as_RB much_RB more_RBR satisfactory_JJ in_IN the_DT case_NN of_IN ganja_NN and_CC bhang_NN than_IN in_IN the_DT case_NN of_IN charas_NNS ._.
